{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-09-28 00:55:18","updatedTime":"2021-09-28 00:55:18","title":"MISC Studio Creates Relationships Between People + Space","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=453231","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/misc-studio-creates-relationships-between-people-space/misc-studio-klassiker-chair-5/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/06/MISC-Studio-Klassiker-Chair-5-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"MISC Studio Creates Relationships Between People + Space\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Based in Seoul, South Korea, <strong><a href=\"https://misc.kr/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">MISC Studio</a> </strong>is helmed by an artist and a designer exploring the relationship between people and space. Their end goal is to create interaction beyond language, through visuals alone. Today we&#8217;re sharing their latest, a furniture retrospective on traditional Korean culture that&#8217;s been modernized. An accompanying modern dance performance – the Living Performance Project – focuses on the emotions formed by the perception of the Klassiker lounge chair and SEOULBAN side table they&#8217;ve created. The viewer is then immersed in the furniture and its design.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=453295\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-453295\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-453295\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/06/MISC-Studio-Klassiker-Chair-2-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"brown chair\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/06/MISC-Studio-Klassiker-Chair-2-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/06/MISC-Studio-Klassiker-Chair-2-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/06/MISC-Studio-Klassiker-Chair-2-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/06/MISC-Studio-Klassiker-Chair-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>MISC Studio&#8217;s <a href=\"https://misc.kr/Klassiker\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Klassiker</a> is a lounge chair inspired by the traditional Korean A-frame carrier: ji-gae. Klassiker is designed to support weight with a simple system, the tension of the extended front and rear legs, along with the stability of oval-shaped wooden support, create a perfect balance. The A-frame structure on the back of the Klassiker is designed to be durable and express the classical ji-gae structure.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_453300\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=453300\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-453300\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-453300\" 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">ji-gae (Korean A-frame) is a traditional Korean carrier used to efficiently transport heavy objects through weight distribution.</p></div>\n<p><a 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The <a href=\"https://misc.kr/seoulban\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">SEOULBAN</a> side table reinterprets a Korean dining table used since 37 A.D. through today. Functionality is improved with the more compact size, its simplicity marks the old days of Seoul. Inspired by Susunjeondo, an old map portraying Hanyang (old Seoul) during the Joseon Dynasty, SEOULBAN puts forth a modernized dining table linked to traditional furniture. The boundary of Seoul is marked with a heavy squared wooden top with curved edges. Molding details around the table&#8217;s base signify the eight castle gates that surrounded Seoul.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_453307\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a Gala","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=460842","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><em>Every other week we’re inviting one of the Design Milk team to share five personal favorites – an opportunity for each of us to reveal the sort of designs we use and appreciate in our own lives from a more personal perspective. Editorial Director <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/author/caroline/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Caroline Williamson</a> returns this week for our <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/tag/take-5/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Take 5</a> series…</em></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/take-5-a-diy-table-retro-keyboard-iman-harris-reed-at-the-met-gala/take5-oct21-calico-wallpaper-atmosphere-daybreak-wallpaper/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Calico-Wallpaper-Atmosphere-Daybreak-Wallpaper-810x703.jpg\" alt=\"Take 5: A DIY Table, Retro Keyboard, Iman + Harris Reed at the Met Gala\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><strong>1. <a href=\"https://calicowallpaper.com/collection/atmosphere/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Atmosphere by Calico Wallpaper</a></strong><br />\nSince Calico Wallpaper launched, they&#8217;ve never had a miss with their designs, and the latest, Atmosphere, continues their upward trajectory. As someone who&#8217;s obsessed with clouds, it&#8217;s impossible not to fall in love with all eight colorways, each depicting the natural shifts of clouds and colors in the sky throughout the day. From Daybreak to Moonlight, they&#8217;re all really beautiful and would make any room feel dreamy.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460845\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460845\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460845\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460845\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Iman-Met-Gala-2021-Harris-Reed-810x1097.jpg\" alt=\"model Iman dressed in gold and feathers at Met Gala\" width=\"810\" height=\"1097\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Iman-Met-Gala-2021-Harris-Reed-810x1097.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Iman-Met-Gala-2021-Harris-Reed-800x1084.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Iman-Met-Gala-2021-Harris-Reed-768x1040.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Iman-Met-Gala-2021-Harris-Reed-1134x1536.jpg 1134w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Iman-Met-Gala-2021-Harris-Reed.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Courtesy Mike Coppola for Getty Images</p></div>\n<p><strong>2. <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/p/CTyZg_4IVZs/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Iman at the Met Gala dressed by Harris Reed</a></strong><br />\nAnother dreamy pick&#8230; Did you catch the Met Gala red carpet, specifically Iman looking like an ethereal golden goddess?! Iman is always stunning, yet she looked even more otherworldly floating along in a gold jacquard bustier and flares with a tiered crinoline and gold leaf overskirt and matching headpiece, all thanks to London-based <a href=\"https://www.harrisreed.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Harris Reed</a>. I&#8217;ve followed the 25-year-old British-American designer on <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/harris_reed/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Instagram</a> for a couple of years now and it&#8217;s no surprise their work landed on a supermodel at the Met Gala. Reed has been nailing each step of a short yet already impressive career which lead to this moment, from a candle collection (I have 2 and they&#8217;re intoxicating), a collaboration with MAC Cosmetics, a line of platform boots with ROKER Atelier, jewelry collaboration with Missoma, and now fresh off the London Fashion Week runway with their demi-couture collection made from upcycled garments from Oxfam. Looking forward to seeing what Reed does next!</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/azio/products/retro-classic-usb?variant=40115067846847\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460847 noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone wp-image-460847 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Azio-Retro-Classic-USB-Keyboard-1-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"angle shot of retro keyboard in maple wood\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Azio-Retro-Classic-USB-Keyboard-1-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Azio-Retro-Classic-USB-Keyboard-1-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Azio-Retro-Classic-USB-Keyboard-1-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Azio-Retro-Classic-USB-Keyboard-1-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Azio-Retro-Classic-USB-Keyboard-1-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Azio-Retro-Classic-USB-Keyboard-1.jpg 1000w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>3. <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/azio/products/retro-classic-usb?variant=40115067846847\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">RETRO CLASSIC USB Keyboard</a></strong><br />\nYes, it&#8217;s super easy to whip open your laptop and start pecking away at the keys conveniently embedded right there. But when you&#8217;re at a desk for any extended period of time, getting a monitor and keyboard is probably a better setup for a multitude of reasons. There are plenty of keyboards to choose from but there&#8217;s something about one with keys that have that tactile clicky thing when pressed. In addition to that super satisfying feature, this keyboard also has a retro look that makes typing much more fun. Plus, it really makes your desk look way cooler than it is.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460848\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460848\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460848\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Faye-Toogood-Cardboard-Roly-Poly-side-table-810x402.jpg\" alt=\"three images showing DIY table made of cardboard\" width=\"810\" height=\"402\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Faye-Toogood-Cardboard-Roly-Poly-side-table-810x402.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Faye-Toogood-Cardboard-Roly-Poly-side-table-800x398.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Faye-Toogood-Cardboard-Roly-Poly-side-table-768x382.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Faye-Toogood-Cardboard-Roly-Poly-side-table.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>4. <a href=\"https://t-o-o-g-o-o-d.com/pages/the-joy-of-cardboard\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Roly-Poly Side Table DIY Instructions from Faye Toogood</a></strong><br />\n<em>The Unboxing Show</em>, which just wrapped at London Design Festival, is an exhibition by designer and artist Peter Marigold, that invited designers to remember that cardboard can be of value despite how much of it goes to waste. Modeled after her Roly-Poly side table, Toogood designed a version to be made from cardboard. At the show, visitors could create the design themselves with the help of a cardboard cutting CNC machine and assistance assembling it from Marigold and his team. If you missed the show, Toogood has <a href=\"https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/1iXMv_Zp2v1b4TgCAAWuVjI77WfGIIG_h\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">released the pattern</a> in two sizes for you to attempt to make it at home.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460849\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460849\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460849\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Paper-Shoot-Paper-Camera-810x571.jpg\" alt=\"paper shot camera opened up\" width=\"810\" height=\"571\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Paper-Shoot-Paper-Camera-810x571.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Paper-Shoot-Paper-Camera-800x564.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Paper-Shoot-Paper-Camera-768x542.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Take5-Oct21-Paper-Shoot-Paper-Camera.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>5. <a href=\"https://papershootcamera.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Paper Shoot Cameras</a></strong><br />\nMany months ago, I started seeing Paper Shoot Cameras popping up on TikTok and became intrigued. I&#8217;ve acquired an army of cameras throughout my life (I have a degree in photography) and always love finding a new one. This camera is the size of a cassette tape (if you&#8217;re old enough to remember those!) and is a legit digital camera that takes photos like a film camera all within a hard paper shell. It runs with two AAA batteries and an SD card, and once installed, you can take photos and videos with a resolution of 13 mega pixels. I ordered this months ago and just received it as they&#8217;ve been on backorder all year. Each meticulously crafted candle is a modern representation of emotion designed to be transformed when lit. You might consider nlumec®’s candles too intricate to burn, but the brand actively invites viewers to light their candles and witness the transformation that takes place. To enjoy the light, you must erase the art.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460520\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/nlumec\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-460520 size-full\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/nlumec_founderimage_810x570.jpg\" alt=\"nlumec candles brand founders \" width=\"810\" height=\"570\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/nlumec_founderimage_810x570.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/nlumec_founderimage_810x570-800x563.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/nlumec_founderimage_810x570-768x540.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Camila Navas and Alex Posadas</p></div>\n<p>Inspired by the creation of light and its role in art and the physical space, nlumec® founders Camila Navas and Alex Posadas explore its relationship to the observer with thoughtfulness and intention. The dynamic connection between light and form is illustrated through the geometric shape of each candle and their hyper-detailed etchings. As the candles burn, the etchings evolve into a delicate, netting-like structure around the candle’s flame. There are 3 unique designs, each named in Latin after an emotional state of being – <strong><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/nlumec/products/gravis\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Gravis</a></strong>, <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/nlumec/products/test_02\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\"><strong>Fortis</strong></a>, and <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/nlumec/products/miratus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\"><strong>Miratus</strong></a> – and laced with different meanings. Composed of materials as fleeting as the emotions themselves, nlumec® candles use a blend of ethically sourced beeswax, with cotton and hemp fibers. The thoughtful spirit and careful construction of nlumec® creations prove that candles can do more than create a warm ambience, they can be mediums of emotional expression through light.</p>\n<p><a It’s your all-important calling card as you share your brand’s story with the world – your future fans, friends, community members and audience.</p>\n<p>It’s a big, important job – and <strong><a href=\"https://share.sqsp.link/designmilk-september-unfoldhomepage\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener sponsored external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Unfold from Squarespace</a></strong> can make it easier than ever to share a beautiful, consistent brand vision across platforms including Instagram, TikTok and Facebook. Unfold provides everything you need to be successful on social media – all within a single app.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460458\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460458\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460458\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-2-810x494.png\" alt=\"side by side phone screen shots of mobile app\" width=\"810\" height=\"494\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-2-810x494.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-2-800x488.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-2-768x468.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-2.png 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Unfold allows you to create stunning, effective content, plan out your posts and present a unified message with a uniquely designed link in bio. Founded three years ago with the mission of making social media stories look every bit as beautiful as top-quality print magazines, Unfold offers a range of innovative features. If you’ve only ever used Instagram’s native tools, you may be amazed at the flexibility Unfold provides, with hundreds of different templates providing unique, high-impact layouts. Unfold offers you a range of stylistic moods and options with a library of super-fashionable fonts, trendy filters and stickers, and the option to upload your own fonts, colors, logos and stickers to apply to your designs with Brand Kit. You won’t need to power up Photoshop or download another photo editing app because it offers a range of professional-caliber filters and effects. Whether you want your images bold and bright or grainy and impressionistic, Unfold can help you achieve precisely the aesthetic your brand – and audience – expect.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460459\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460459\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460459\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-3-810x494.png\" alt=\"side by side images of phone with app on screen and collage of phone screens\" width=\"810\" height=\"494\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-3-810x494.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-3-800x488.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-3-768x468.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-3.png 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The name of the game in social media is to create unique, powerful imagery – that rare creative that’s so striking that it’ll stop a scroll in its tracks. You can do that in seconds with Unfold. If your brand channels 1970s skate culture, you can select a template from the Film Frames that will supply a rough-hewn, Super 8 aesthetic familiar to the early days of skate videos in empty SoCal pools. Meanwhile, the Moodboard collection gives away its fashion-friendly roots in its name. Use it to launch your next collection or showcase your behind-the-scenes inspiration as you bring your latest products to your site.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460460\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460460\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460460\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-4-810x522.png\" alt=\"side by side images of mobile phone screen shots\" width=\"810\" height=\"522\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-4-810x522.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-4-800x516.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-4-768x495.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-4.png 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Another way Unfold can boost your social media is with its Bio Sites feature. Too often, small business’s social impact is diluted because of its inconsistencies across platforms. With Bio Sites, you’ll have a stunning destination for all your “link in bio” clicks – and seamlessly connect new fans with your work wherever you want: on Instagram, Twitter and TikTok or on your own website. Each Bio Site is fully customizable, and you’ll never have to waste time updating your bio links on all your different social media sites again. All you’ll need to do is add your latest news to this one-stop social hub, providing your new fans a hassle-free way to engage with your work.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460461\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460461\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460461\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-5-810x494.png\" alt=\"side by side images of mobile phone screen shots\" width=\"810\" height=\"494\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-5-810x494.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-5-800x488.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-5-768x468.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Squarespace-Unfold-App-5.png 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Outside of your core business offer, one of the most crucial things for your brand’s success is a compelling, consistent, captivating social media presence. 00:55:18","updatedTime":"2021-09-28 00:55:18","title":"The Brizo® Brand’s New Frank Lloyd Wright Bath Collection Expands on Wright’s Iconic Influence","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=460686","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><em>The following post is brought to you by <a href=\"http://brizo.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener sponsored external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Brizo</a>. Our partners are hand-picked by the Design Milk team because they represent the best in design.</em></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/the-brizo-brands-new-frank-lloyd-wright-bath-collection-expands-on-wrights-iconic-influence/frank-lloyd-wright-3/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Featured-Image-810x475.jpg\" alt=\"The Brizo® Brand&#8217;s New Frank Lloyd Wright Bath Collection Expands on Wright&#8217;s Iconic Influence\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><em>Simplicity, individuality, belonging, palette, substance and integrity.</em></p>\n<p>Frank Lloyd Wright’s six principles of organic architecture and design philosophy have found a new home in the new <a href=\"https://bit.ly/FLWbyBrizo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener sponsored external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><strong>Frank Lloyd Wright</strong>®<strong> Bath Collection by Brizo</strong>®</a>. The architect’s artistry and influence can be felt in every piece of the bathroom suite, from a cantilevered spout design that seems to defy gravity to the side-stream water flow that challenges traditional design. Created in collaboration with the <a href=\"http://FrankLloydWright.org\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener sponsored external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><strong>Frank Lloyd Wright Foundation</strong></a>, this is a forward-looking collection that pays homage to Wright’s work and helps advance his design legacy long into the future.</p>\n<p>“We have been honored to work with the Frank Lloyd Wright Foundation as we developed and designed this collection,” said Judd Lord, Senior Director of Industrial Design. “Their dedication to create and inspire in the name of making life more beautiful mirrors our own steadfast commitment to inspire, challenge and elevate the world around us through distinctive design and unparalleled craftsmanship. Staying true to Frank Lloyd Wright’s vision of reinvention was core to our product development, and the Foundation’s incredible knowledge and deep reverence for that vision has been invaluable.”</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460691\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460691\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460691\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460691\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Rectangular-Raincan-Showerhead-810x900.jpg\" alt=\"rectangular showerhead with light and water turned on\" width=\"810\" height=\"900\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Rectangular-Raincan-Showerhead-810x900.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Rectangular-Raincan-Showerhead-800x889.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Rectangular-Raincan-Showerhead-768x853.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Rectangular-Raincan-Showerhead.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Rectangular Raincan Showerhead</p></div>\n<p>Inspired by Wright’s encompassing oeuvre, and pulling from the natural world he gravitated toward, the collection exhibits his revolutionary style of American architecture through carefully chosen materials and meticulous attention to detail. Within the collection, metal finishes bring in an elemental tone that, when paired with wood, feels warm and intuitive. You’ll find that innovation runs throughout with notable details including the Single-Function Raincan Showerhead with Integrated Lighting,  showcasing the Canopy Spray with an activating, built-in light for a dramatic effect.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460692\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460692\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460692\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460692\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Single-Handle-Lavatory-Faucet-810x1131.jpg\" alt=\"wood and metal angular sink faucet with water turned on\" width=\"810\" height=\"1131\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Single-Handle-Lavatory-Faucet-810x1131.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Single-Handle-Lavatory-Faucet-800x1117.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Single-Handle-Lavatory-Faucet-768x1072.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Single-Handle-Lavatory-Faucet-1100x1536.jpg 1100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Single-Handle-Lavatory-Faucet.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Single Handle Lavatory Faucet</p></div>\n<blockquote><p>The cantilevered spout featured in a few of the collection’s core pieces is a powerhouse design that showcases water as a central design element. I hope that would’ve been Wright’s favorite of the collection as the cantilevered spout water has an unorthodox water flow, which streams from the side. It directly channels Wright’s artistry as someone who challenged conventions.</p></blockquote>\n<p><em>– Lucia McBroom, Brizo Senior Brand Manager</em></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460694\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460694\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460694\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460694\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Widespread-Lavatory-Faucet-810x475.jpg\" alt=\"double vanity bathroom sink with wood and metal sink faucets\" width=\"810\" height=\"475\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Widespread-Lavatory-Faucet-810x475.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Widespread-Lavatory-Faucet-800x469.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Widespread-Lavatory-Faucet-768x450.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Widespread-Lavatory-Faucet.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Widespread Lavatory Faucet</p></div>\n<p>“People sometimes make the mistake of thinking Frank Lloyd Wright’s legacy is complete,” said Stuart Graff, President and CEO of the Frank Lloyd Wright Foundation. “But really, it’s ongoing. It’s not just about what he created in his lifetime – it’s about all the artists and all the disciplines he inspired and their work going forward. That’s why working with the Brizo brand has been such a delight. They understand that honoring Frank Lloyd Wright’s vision means continuing it. And in this collection, they have.”</p>\n<p>The <a href=\"http://FrankLloydWright.org\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener sponsored external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Frank Lloyd Wright Foundation</a> was established in 1940 by Wright himself. Their dedication lies in preserving Taliesin and Taliesin West, both UNESCO Heritage sites, and bringing inspiration to others to discover architecture for better, more meaningful living through nature and the arts. The Foundation carries on his legacy by allowing broader access to his ideas, works and designs so that others might create and connect in their own lives.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460693\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460693\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460693\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460693\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Two-Handle-Floor-Mount-Tub-Filler-and-Accessory-Kit-810x1252.jpg\" alt=\"metal floor mount bathtub faucet\" width=\"810\" height=\"1252\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Two-Handle-Floor-Mount-Tub-Filler-and-Accessory-Kit-810x1252.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Two-Handle-Floor-Mount-Tub-Filler-and-Accessory-Kit-800x1236.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Two-Handle-Floor-Mount-Tub-Filler-and-Accessory-Kit-768x1187.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Two-Handle-Floor-Mount-Tub-Filler-and-Accessory-Kit-994x1536.jpg 994w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brizo-Frank-Lloyd-Wright-Bathroom-Collection-Two-Handle-Floor-Mount-Tub-Filler-and-Accessory-Kit.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Two Handle Floor Mount Tub Filler</p></div>\n<p>To provide a firsthand look into his legacy, a virtual showroom showcases the collection’s unique design elements and functionality. To explore the showroom, visit <a href=\"https://bit.ly/BrizoShowroom\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener sponsored external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">brizo.com/frank-lloyd-wright/virtual-showroom/</a>.</p>\n<p>The Frank Lloyd Wright Bath Collection includes a full suite of lavatory faucets, tub fillers and spouts, shower components and accessories. Choose from six available finishes, including Polished Chrome, <em>Brilliance</em>® Polished Nickel, <em>Brilliance</em>® Luxe Nickel®, <em>Brilliance</em>® Luxe Steel®, <em>Brilliance</em>® Polished Nickel/Wood and <em>Brilliance</em>® Luxe Nickel®/Wood.</p>\n<p>This visionary collection is available through luxury kitchen and bath showrooms throughout North America. 00:55:18","updatedTime":"2021-09-28 00:55:18","title":"Empathic. Discovering a Glass Legacy Explores the Powers of Matter + Shape","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=460530","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/empathic-discovering-a-glass-legacy-explores-the-powers-of-matter-shape/empathic-discovery-a-glass-legacy-noe-duchaufour-lawrance-madonna-del-monte-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-Featured-Image-810x475.jpg\" alt=\"Empathic. Discovering a Glass Legacy Explores the Powers of Matter + Shape\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><strong>Luca Nichetto</strong>, curator of the fourth exhibition at InGalleria, the Art Gallery of <a href=\"https://puntaconterie.com/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Punta Conterie</a> a Murano in Venice, chose an adjective as part of the name for the show. <em>Empathic</em>. The ability to share a feeling with others, in this case through the powers of matter and shape. Through April 10, 2022, installations and limited edition pieces by Ini Archibong, Noé Duchaufour-Lawrance, GamFratesi, Benjamin Hubert, Richard Hutten, Luca Nichetto, Elena Salmistraro and Marc Thorpe will be on display for <strong>Empathic. Discovering a Glass Legacy</strong>.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460554\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460554\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460554\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460554\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-1-810x853.jpg\" alt=\"grey coffee table and grey side table on white background\" width=\"810\" height=\"853\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-1-810x853.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-1-800x843.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-1-768x809.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Madonna Del Monte by Noe Duchaufour Lawrence</p></div>\n<p>Noé Duchaufour-Lawrance found inspiration in shades used in the photographic series “Down by the water” by photographer Lucie Jean that&#8217;s focused on a small island in the Venice Lagoon called Madonna del Monte. The result is a series of small sized furnishings and sculptures of the same name.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460555\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460555\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460555\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460555\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-Sketch-810x854.jpg\" alt=\"color sketch of glass table design\" width=\"810\" height=\"854\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-Sketch-810x854.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-Sketch-800x844.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-Sketch-768x810.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Noe-Duchaufour-Lawrance-Madonna-Del-Monte-Sketch.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Madonna Del Monte by Noe Duchaufour Lawrence</p></div>\n<p>Nichetto, who also has an installation on display, invited the individuals to freely incorporate Murano glass into their works. No brief or constraints, only freedom to design and experiment with blown glass, glass rods and cast glass. Empathic. Discovering a Glass Legacy combines the craftsmanship of talented Murano glassworkers, each specializing in a specific glass working technique, with the pure creativity of the designers involved. The resulting installations and editions showcase the magic that can occur when master and designer work together to convey emotion, perception and more.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460557\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460557\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460557\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460557\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Richard-Hutten-Layered-1-810x1072.jpg\" alt=\"tower-like sculpture with striated banks of color\" width=\"810\" height=\"1072\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Richard-Hutten-Layered-1-810x1072.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Richard-Hutten-Layered-1-768x1016.jpg 768w, Richard Hutten</p></div>\n<p>Richard Hutten experimented with color overlays and verticality in his Layered totem that&#8217;s stratified, varied and intense.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460558\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460558\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460558\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460558\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Richard-Hutten-Layered-Sketch-810x1146.jpg\" alt=\"sketch of a tower-like sculpture with striated banks of color\" width=\"810\" height=\"1146\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Richard-Hutten-Layered-Sketch-810x1146.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Richard-Hutten-Layered-Sketch-800x1132.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Richard-Hutten-Layered-Sketch-768x1087.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Richard-Hutten-Layered-Sketch-1086x1536.jpg 1086w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Richard-Hutten-Layered-Sketch.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Layered by Richard Hutten</p></div>\n<blockquote><p>I hope that all the energy dedicated to Empathic will bring a positive message of growth and broadening of horizons; I hope that this exhibition is able to involve and entice young designers to work and draw inspiration from the great little reality of Murano.</p></blockquote>\n<p><em>– Luca Nichetto</em></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460553\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460553\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460553\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460553\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Marc-Thorpe-La-Famiglia-1-810x586.jpg\" alt=\"five striped murano glass vessels on a white background\" https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Marc-Thorpe-La-Famiglia-1-768x556.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Marc-Thorpe-La-Famiglia-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">La Famiglia by Marc Thorpe</p></div>\n<p>Marc Thorpe looked to the Venetian lagoon to create a collection of blown glass objects of various vertically striped shapes named The Family.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460542\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460542\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460542\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460542\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Marc-Thorpe-La-Famiglia-Sketch-810x941.jpg\" alt=\"blue and grey sketch of three tall vessels\" width=\"810\" height=\"941\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Marc-Thorpe-La-Famiglia-Sketch-810x941.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Marc-Thorpe-La-Famiglia-Sketch.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">La Famiglia by Marc Thorpe</p></div>\n<p><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.13px;\">The exhibition, produced by InGalleria Art Gallery under the direction of Alessandro Vecchiato, investigates and crosses boundaries through the give and take of the glass. </span>“Asking Luca Nichetto to conceive and curate this exhibition, I wanted to see what would happen if we all got involved by experimenting, disrupting the grammar of the forms, techniques and ingenuity of each to reach unprecedented results.&#8221;</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460543\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460543\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460543\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460543\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Benjamin-Hubert-Granule-1-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"three multicolored glass bowls/vessels on white background\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Benjamin-Hubert-Granule-1-810x540.jpg 810w, Benjamin Hubert</p></div>\n<p>Benjamin Hubert observed the skills of Murano glass masters to design Granule, a series of objects in which chromatic gradients mark the different shapes and textures of glass: smooth, satin, melted, in granules.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460544\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460544\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460544\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Empathic-Discovery-a-Glass-Legacy-Benjamin-Hubert-Granule-Sketch-810x810.jpg 810w, by Benjamin Hubert</p></div>\n<p>Nichetto summarized, “I believe that the beauty of Empathic cannot be expressed by a single piece, but by the fact that the creation process had the sole intention of supporting Murano glass. And I like to think that we too are part of the rich tradition of designers who have worked with Murano glass over the years.”</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460549\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460549\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460549\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460549\" Nichetto</p></div>\n<p>Luca Nichetto, no stranger to Murano glass, used childhood tales, such as Goldrake, to bring Mecha to life. Three small colorful glass robots evoke icons in rustproof and glittering armor.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460552\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a 00:55:18","updatedTime":"2021-09-28 00:55:18","title":"Domino’s Kate Berry On Designing Honestly + Intuitively For Crate&Kids","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=460593","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/dominos-kate-berry-on-designing-honestly-intuitively-for-cratekids/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-2/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-2-810x630.jpg\" alt=\"Domino&#8217;s Kate Berry On Designing Honestly + Intuitively For Crate&#038;Kids\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>If you didn’t know <strong>Kate Berry</strong> but just started following her <a href=\"https://instagram.com/kateberryberry\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">Instagram</a>, you would have thought she was a born and bred New Yorker, with her fabulous rooftop soirees, weekend farmers market jaunts, and insider knowledge of NYC dining culture that should only come after years of living in the city. However, the Chief Creative Officer at Domino actually hails from Southern California, and it was here that she turned to for inspiration when designing <a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><strong>Domino’s new collaboration with Crate&#38;Kids</strong></a>. The line of children’s furniture, bedding accessories and room decor is bright and punchy, a design direction that meets at the intersections of Domino’s aesthetic, kids’ preferences, and the ‘80s surf and art culture that Berry grew up with.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone wp-image-460598 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-5-810x630.jpg\" alt=\"modern kids room with colorful furniture\" width=\"810\" height=\"630\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-5-810x630.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-5-800x622.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-5-768x597.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-5.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone wp-image-460594 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-1-810x630.jpg\" alt=\"modern kids room with blue and yellow theme\" width=\"810\" height=\"630\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-1-810x630.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-1-800x622.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-1-768x597.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>But designing children’s furniture is more than just nailing down the color palette and sizing the furniture correctly. As it turns out, Berry drew upon honesty, her childhood, and her experience as a mother raising her daughter in NYC to inform her of this collaboration, as Kate Berry explains in a recent chat with Design Milk:</p>\n<p><strong>The Domino aesthetic is very specific and very special, but how would you describe it when you brought it over to a furniture line?</strong></p>\n<p>Crate&#38;Barrel had never worked with a publisher and said, we really love Domino’s sense of color *and* your design is accessible.</p>\n<p>A lot of the stories we do are not necessarily the highest design. We range, we have some places that we shoot that are very aspiration and I love those, but we also shoot small studio apartments. Maybe some people have really amazing art and furniture, and some people have IKEA hacks that are very clever and smart, so I think they really wanted to work with us for that accessibility and relatability.</p>\n<p>With that in mind, we emphasized on small space. Kids furniture, they make little because they’re kids, but when I think about small space, it’s not about smaller furniture. Actually, a lot of the furniture is big, but it maximizes the space, so going up higher. I really pushed for a bookshelf to be super tall, like why does it have to be this [shorter] height? If we’re talking about small space, we want to maximize.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone wp-image-460614 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-17-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"colorful modern bookshelf for kids\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-17-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-17-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-17-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-17-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-17.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460596\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-3-810x630.jpg\" alt=\"kids furniture\" width=\"810\" height=\"630\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-3-810x630.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-3-800x622.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-3-768x597.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-3.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>Or else it’s just lost space.</strong></p>\n<p>Exactly. So that was the mentality. We made things that are a bit taller. So it was accessible design, color, and emphasis on small spaces.</p>\n<p>What was very important to me was sustainability and modular design. Modular and sustainable meaning, I didn’t want to have something where, once you’re 11, you’re done with it. I wanted this furniture to grow with you.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone wp-image-460615 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-18-810x1214.jpg\" alt=\"kids blue and wood art cart on wheels\" width=\"810\" height=\"1214\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-18-810x1214.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-18-800x1199.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-18-768x1151.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-18-1025x1536.jpg 1025w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-18.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone wp-image-460604 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-7-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"kids modern art studio with art cart and modern rug\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-7-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-7-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-7-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-7.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460613\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-16-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"kids bookshelf\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-16-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-16-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-16-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-16-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-16.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>That was going to be my next question for you. Kids furniture is usually very colorful. I think Domino brings a very optimistic color palette to the collection, which I love. Personally as a mom, I’m always grappling with, do I invest in furniture that can grow with them until they’re teenagers or do I want to preserve them in their childhood moment? Does it need to grow with them or do you think kids furniture should have its own special moment on the timeline of furniture that they’re going to have?</strong></p>\n<p>That’s a good question. This is how we tackled that. The furniture should grow with you, most certainly, but what a three- to four-year-old wants versus what a teenager wants is going to be totally different. So the way we imagined it is modularity. There’s a bookshelf, it’s a neutral bookshelf, you can take that to college, you can have that in your living room when they’re grown. But there are these colorful boxes that you can fit and slide in. My daughter Quinn has so many LEGO and plastic toys so you can either throw them in, slide them, and they’re these color blocks, or you can flip them on the other side and they’re shelves so you can put paperwork.</p>\n<p>The furniture, definitely. To me, I didn’t want it to be a wasteful thing that you would throw out. This has got to work for a teenager.</p>\n<p>The bedding is where we definitely had this push and pull because I wanted just stripes and things that <em>I</em> would want to live with. But Sebastian (Brauer, VP of Product Design at Crate&#38;Barrel) said, “Here me out. Kids really need something to identify with.”</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460597\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-4-810x630.jpg\" alt=\"kids furniture\" width=\"810\" height=\"630\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-4-810x630.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-4-800x622.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-4-768x597.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-4.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em>Kate Berry tapped on her artist friends to create some of the familiar figurative and graphic elements that kids would be able to recognize. San Francisco-based graphic artist and surfer Jeff Canham injected fun and playfulness with a glow-in-the-dark, reversible quilt and a Suns, Swims, Seas print that reads the same way upside down. Further down in Los Angeles, Mary Matson adds a whimsical and electric style with surfer cushions and a wavy, beach-reminiscent quilt.</em></p>\n<p>I showed these things to my daughter and some of my friends’ kids’, boys and girls, different in ages. The kids really gravitated towards certain figurative things! So I said, “OK. You guys are the experts.” So there are those moments that are just for the young kids.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460618\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-21-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"kids bedding\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-21-810x540.jpg 810w, 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-21.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-22-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-22-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-22-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-22.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460617\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-20-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"kids bedding\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-20-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-20-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-20-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-20.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>At least the main furniture, the things that the parents are investing in, will definitely grow with them, and the items that are a little lower of a price point are the things they can switch out as they grow older.</strong></p>\n<p>Yeah, like bedding. You probably are not going to have the same bedding for 10 years. Maybe! But really, you want the furniture to last, so that’s what our thinking was behind that.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460608\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-11-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"kids furniture\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-11-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-11-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-11-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-11.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460606\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-9-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"kids trundle bed\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-9-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-9-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-9-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-9-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-9.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em>In thinking about storage, Kate Berry leaned on her experience as a mom to her 8-year-old daughter Quinn, a budding creative and artist in her own right who holds the special items in her life so dearly. With the trundle bed and soft storage containers made to fit it perfectly, there can be a home for everything.</em></p>\n<p>Those were specifically designed because of the need I have as a mother. My daughter has all these trinkets that are so special to her. This will happen to you. It happens to every parent I know. You’re going to go in and try edit and get rid of their things. Don’t try to do it when they’re home. They will dig it out of the garbage and go “This is so special to me!”</p>\n<p>Having these different compartments and things that are accessible to them, my hope is that we’ll give them the tools to be autonomous and be able to organize for themselves where they want to organize. We have a nightstand that has a bulletin board. My daughter makes a lot of art, so to be able to pin that up next to her bed and have her art around her, it’s very important for the way our family lives. I’m going off on a tangent…</p>\n<p><strong>No, that’s actually my next question which was how did your role as a mom inform you of these design decisions? It seems like you made sure that kids, even though they’re kids, they have autonomy over their own space and they can curate and grow. All day long they’re told to do things and, in their own safe space that you’ve created for them, they can express themselves, even if they’re two or eight years old.</strong></p>\n<p>You can give them these things and you can give them the space, but you’re also kind of teaching them to organize at an early age. However they do it, if they do it or not, it’s their space to do whatever they choose to do with it.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460605\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-8-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"kids furniture\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-8-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-8-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-8-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-8.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460609\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-12-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"kids furniture\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-12-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-12-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-12-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-12.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em>While Kate Berry admits that her own childhood had limited options when it came to kids furniture (she creatively fashioned a vanity from a milk crate and some leftover fabric for her rainbow pinstripe wallpapered room), she is able to draw upon her past in recognizing the importance of designing pieces that, ultimately, needs to make kids feel safe and right at home.</em></p>\n<p>I didn’t have these kinds of choices! I had a Smurf bedspread and I loved it so much. It made me think, oh okay, these figurative things are going to make you want to sleep in your bed. You have to make things that kids are actually going to like, because they have to like it and they have to feel comfortable especially in the bed.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460610\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-13-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"kids desk\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-13-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-13-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-13-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-13-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-13.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em>It&#8217;s clear that any kid or teenager can find delight in the new collection, but while the furniture and fun accessories can help them become more organized and provide autonomy over their own space, Kate Berry knows that it&#8217;s just one of the many lessons we as parents are responsible for in raising our kids.</em></p>\n<p>There are people that teach their kids to be polite and have manners, but I want Quinn to understand why she’s saying thank you to the cab driver. I tell her, &#8220;He’s leaving his family, risking his life, making our lives easier, so it’s very important for you to understand that.&#8221; She knows why she’s thanking people.</p>\n<p><strong>I’m working on that myself with my daughter Nora.</strong></p>\n<p>I’m still working on it, we’ll always be working on it, as honest as we can be with them. I think that’s what’s important. I was trying that with this furniture line, to be really real about it and know what parents need.</p>\n<p><strong>I think honesty is what really informed your decisions, along with the Domino aesthetic. With your life as a mom and what your kid needs, and in considering what parents need, I think honesty came through with this collection.</strong></p>\n<p>Well, thank you!</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3tZXsp4\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460616\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-19-810x752.jpg\" alt=\"kids room\" width=\"810\" height=\"752\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-19-810x752.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-19-800x743.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-19-768x713.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/cratekids-domino-collaboration-kate-berry-19.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em>This post contains affiliate links, so if you make a purchase from an affiliate link, we earn a commission. sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Frampton Co.</p></div>\n<p><em>Interior designer and art advisor <strong>Elena Frampton</strong> is the founder and principal of <strong><a href=\"https://www.framptonco.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Frampton Co.</a></strong> With locations in New York City and Bridgehampton, the firm designs and creates interior experiences, specializing in interior architecture, design and art advisement. Elena&#8217;s design approach is instinctual from the get-go. She reads a client&#8217;s latent desires for their space, bringing to life environments that they themselves didn&#8217;t yet know they wanted. Elena&#8217;s work gives shape and feeling to visions for where and how we live.</em></p>\n<p><em>Frampton Co.&#8217;s portfolio includes residences, select commercial projects and F Collection private label furnishings. You can find the latter on view alongside other curated artworks for purchase in gallery settings at <a href=\"https://www.framptonco.com/show/exhibition-the-barn/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Exhibition The Barn</a> in Bridgehampton and <a href=\"https://www.framptonco.com/exhibition/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Exhibition Penthouse</a> in NYC.</em></p>\n<p><em>Today Elena joins us for <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/column/friday-five/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Friday Five</a>!</em></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460282\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460282\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460282\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460282\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Sag-Harbor-Photo-Frampton-Co-810x1080.jpg\" alt=\"white puppy wearing a leash on the beach\" width=\"810\" height=\"1080\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Sag-Harbor-Photo-Frampton-Co-810x1080.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Sag-Harbor-Photo-Frampton-Co-800x1067.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Sag-Harbor-Photo-Frampton-Co-768x1024.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Sag-Harbor-Photo-Frampton-Co-1152x1536.jpg 1152w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Sag-Harbor-Photo-Frampton-Co.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Elena Frampton</p></div>\n<p><strong>1. Sag Harbor Beach Walks</strong><br />\nLiving in Bridgehampton, I’m surrounded by dynamic ocean beaches and peaceful bays. My favorite morning ritual is to take my puppy Vesper for a long brisk walk at Long Beach in Sag Harbor. Located on a thin strip of land on Noyac Bay, it’s a beautiful spot for contemplation… and exercise when Vesper has me running! Beyond the water, birds and seascape, every now and again I’ll run into a familiar face.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460283\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460283\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460283\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460283\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Shore-Rug-Photo-Future-Perfect-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"multicolored striped rug on pavement\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Shore-Rug-Photo-Future-Perfect-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Shore-Rug-Photo-Future-Perfect-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Shore-Rug-Photo-Future-Perfect-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Shore-Rug-Photo-Future-Perfect.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: <a href=\"https://www.thefutureperfect.com/made-by/manufacturer/shore-rugs/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">The Future Perfect</a></p></div>\n<p><strong>2. Shore Rugs<br />\n</strong>These soft, made-for-bare-feet rugs are wonderful. We’re always on the hunt for brands that create durable and stylish indoor-outdoor solutions, and <a href=\"https://shorerugs.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Shore Rugs</a> fit the bill. Why shouldn’t our outdoor spaces be as colorful and layered as our indoor spaces? No off-the-shelf outdoor furniture sets here! No matchy-matchy! These rugs bring a uniquely energetic aesthetic to spaces.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460280\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460280\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460280\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460280\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Howard-Kanovitz-Photo-Frampton-Co-810x958.jpg\" alt=\"decorated nook with light walls, artwork, and vase of flowers\" width=\"810\" height=\"958\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Howard-Kanovitz-Photo-Frampton-Co-810x958.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Howard-Kanovitz-Photo-Frampton-Co-800x946.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Howard-Kanovitz-Photo-Frampton-Co-768x908.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Howard-Kanovitz-Photo-Frampton-Co.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Elena Frampton</p></div>\n<p><strong>3. Artwork by Howard Kanovitz</strong><br />\n<a href=\"https://www.howardkanovitz.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Howard Kanovitz</a> was a mid-century photorealist painter who lived and worked in New York City and in the Hamptons. His airbrush technique and distinct vision is reflected in Hamptons Drive-In (1974), one of my favorite artworks in my own home. It feels like my own little slice of Hamptons art history – the actual Drive-In movie theater opened in 1955, just down the street. A much larger version of this artwork is a part of the permanent collection at the nearby Parrish Art Museum in Water Mill.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460285\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460285\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460285\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460285\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Taos-Photo-Frampton-Co-810x608.jpg\" alt=\"desert landscape with wide blue sky\" width=\"810\" height=\"608\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Taos-Photo-Frampton-Co-810x608.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Taos-Photo-Frampton-Co-800x600.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Taos-Photo-Frampton-Co-768x576.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Taos-Photo-Frampton-Co.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Elena Frampton</p></div>\n<p><strong>4. Taos, New Mexico</strong><br />\nI often venture to the southwest for respite. I love Taos, New Mexico for its clear air, ample space for reflection, long hikes and its mysterious nature of spirituality. Desert landscapes hold a very special place in my heart and Taos has been the source of a lot of personal growth. I bring the energy it gives me back to New York. It’s part of what powers my creative practice, and what I bring into my thinking about spaces in conceptual ways and the energy in them.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460278\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460278\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460278\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-460278\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Berry-Campbell-Photo-Frampton-Co-810x608.jpg\" alt=\"art gallery with white walls and three abstract paintings\" width=\"810\" height=\"608\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Berry-Campbell-Photo-Frampton-Co-810x608.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Berry-Campbell-Photo-Frampton-Co-800x600.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Berry-Campbell-Photo-Frampton-Co-768x576.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/F5-Elena-Hampton-Berry-Campbell-Photo-Frampton-Co.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Elena Frampton</p></div>\n<p><strong>5. Berry Campbell<br />\n</strong>One of my go-to galleries in New York City is <a href=\"https://www.berrycampbell.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Berry Campbell</a> – great art works, friendly atmosphere and an inspiring robust program! The gallery champions female painters like Yvonne Thomas, Perle Fine and Judith Godwin, giving women artists long overdue consideration on the market. They also represent a diverse range of works with something for everyone: from minimalist Walter Darby Bannard, to the more expressive William Perehudoff, to the very geometric Ken Greenleaf. I can also spend forever perusing their online inventory – a convenience especially now.</p>\n<p><em><strong>Work by Frampton Co.:</strong></em></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460284\" class=\"wp-caption
