Furniture","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=460074","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/brigette-romanek-x-mitchell-gold-bob-williams-create-curvaceous-furniture/brigette-romanek-x-mitchell-gold-bob-williams-furniture-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-Featured-Image-810x477.jpg\" alt=\"Brigette Romanek x Mitchell Gold + Bob Williams Create Curvaceous Furniture\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>This furniture collaboration has curves and sophistication for days, and we have interior designer <a href=\"https://romanekdesignstudio.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Brigette Romanek</a> and <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/furniture\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">furniture</a> brand <a href=\"https://www.mgbwhome.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Mitchell Gold + Bob Williams</a> to thank for it. Romanek&#8217;s client roster includes Beyonce and Jay-Z, Gwyneth Paltrow and Misty Copeland, among others, so she&#8217;s no stranger to creating environments that are comfortable and beautiful. She refers to it as &#8220;livable luxe&#8221;, and that&#8217;s exactly the bullseye that the <a href=\"https://www.mgbwhome.com/new/brigette-romanek-x-mgbw/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><strong>Brigette Romanek x Mitchell Gold + Bob Williams</strong></a> collaboration hits dead-on.</p>\n<p>This 7-piece collection is Romanek&#8217;s first foray into furniture design, but Mitchell Gold + Bob Williams are pros. (They just expanded into a full lifestyle brand earlier this year!). The two parties make for a great pair, standing for quality American craftsmanship, sustainability and diversity.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460084\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460084\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460084\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-2-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"white living space with sofa, armchairs, coffee table, and two dogs\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-2-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-2-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-2-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The collection&#8217;s designs were inspired by Romanek&#8217;s life in Los Angeles with her husband, two daughters and two dogs. Her desire to make each piece feel functional and cozy was made possible by MGBW adjusting details to create comfortable pieces with a bit of modern whimsy. Romanek and MGBW&#8217;s collaboration includes two micro collections and a standalone piece.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460085\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460085\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460085\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-3-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"turquoise chair in front of large bookcase\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-3-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-3-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-3-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-3-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-3.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The Lucy Collection holds a sofa, chair and right or left daybed, balancing architecture, fashion and art deco through its two rows of cushioning. Round pillows and angled wood legs add the perfect touch. The L.A. Collection features a chair, ottoman, two sizes of sofas and an upholstered bed with oversized, hand-tailored cushions as its hallmark. All upholstery is available for customization with hundreds of fabrics and 20+ MGBW wood finishes. Lastly, there&#8217;s the Dell Swivel Chair. A classic that&#8217;s been perfectly scaled, it&#8217;s made up of a lower back, angled arms and a wood swivel base before being topped off with a round cushion. It comes in your choice of hundreds of fabrics and leathers.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460086\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460086\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460086\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/Brigette-Romanek-x-Mitchell-Gold-Bob-Williams-Furniture-4-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"pink sofa, turquoise chair, white bench, and coffee table in light room with a wall of books\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" 00:55:18","updatedTime":"2021-09-28 00:55:18","title":"Supporting Women and Saving the World One Bag at a Time","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=460706","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/supporting-women-and-saving-the-world-one-bag-at-a-time/junes_brandspotlight_featuredimage_grandetote-1280x720/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_featuredimage_grandetote-1280x720-1-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"Supporting Women and Saving the World One Bag at a Time\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Meet <a title=\"Junes\" href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\"><strong>Junes</strong></a>. The reusable bag company that’s doing its part to solve the world&#8217;s plastic problem, and support women across the globe. For founder Janean Mann, the solution to the cycle of plastic pollution was simple: create the ultimate reusable bag, and make it something people want to use again and again. Their compact design, stylish colors, and accessible price points already make <a title=\"Junes bags\" href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Junes bags</a> winners in our book. The brand didn’t stop there.</p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When Mann visited Juarez, Mexico, she partnered with a local, all-women sewing co-op to produce its bags, weaving support for women into the brand’s fabric. The partnership helps women of Juarez achieve economic autonomy while supporting their families. The company continues proving its commitment to women at a global scale by donating a portion of every sale to the Global Fund for Women, a non-profit foundation empowering and protecting women around the world through human right’s initiatives.</span></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460708\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-460708 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_juarezco-op-1280x900-1-810x570.jpg\" alt=\"Junes all woman sewing co-op in juarez, mexico\" width=\"810\" height=\"570\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_juarezco-op-1280x900-1-810x570.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_juarezco-op-1280x900-1-800x563.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_juarezco-op-1280x900-1-768x540.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_juarezco-op-1280x900-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Junes’ partnership with an all-female sewing co-op in Juarez, Mexico provides a sustainable income for women along our shared border.</p></div>\n<p>In an effort to close the loop on plastic pollution, Junes makes every decision with the planet&#8217;s future in mind. Their signature Bio-Knit mesh material combines existing, recycled plastics with CiCLO®, a revolutionary technology that allows naturally occurring microbes in landfills or sea water to consume the material (ensuring the bags won’t last forever if they end up in a landfill or waterway).</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_460709\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-460709 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_grandebag-1280x720-1-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"a yellow junes grande bag with a yoga mat and other essentials inside\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_grandebag-1280x720-1-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_grandebag-1280x720-1-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_grandebag-1280x720-1-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_grandebag-1280x720-1-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_brandspotlight_grandebag-1280x720-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">All Junes bags are made with their signature Bio-Knit material &#8211; a durable mesh made from recycled plastics.</p></div>\n<p>Junes&#8217; innovative material not only changes the future of textiles as we know it, but it also makes their <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">bags</a> even more durable, so you can enjoy your Junes bag for years to come. Plus, they&#8217;re machine washable and get softer over time without losing firmness. When you’re done loving your bag, send it back to be shredded, melted and recycled into new yarn for another Junes bag through their #TradeUpJunes program. Pretty cool huh?</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes/products/the-everyday-tote-in-bioknit\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone wp-image-460711 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_everydaytote_1280x900-810x570.jpg\" alt=\"person carrying a white junes everyday tote over their shoulder with produce and other things inside\" width=\"810\" height=\"570\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_everydaytote_1280x900-810x570.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_everydaytote_1280x900-800x563.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_everydaytote_1280x900-768x540.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_everydaytote_1280x900.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a title=\"The Everyday Tote\" href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes/products/the-everyday-tote-in-bioknit\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\"><strong>The Everyday Tote</strong></a><br />\nThe original Junes bag, the Everyday Tote is a universal favorite. The tote uses Junes’ signature Bio-knit material and is available in a variety of colors, so you never have to sacrifice style for sustainability. Fit with two deep inner pockets for your wallet, keys and water bottle, the Everyday Tote can go anywhere you do.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes/products/carry-alls-in-bio-knit\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone wp-image-460710 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_carryallset_1280x900-810x570.jpg\" alt=\"junes white carry all set with books, and other small things inside\" width=\"810\" height=\"570\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_carryallset_1280x900-810x570.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_carryallset_1280x900-800x563.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_carryallset_1280x900-768x540.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_carryallset_1280x900.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a title=\"The Carry-All Set\" href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes/products/carry-alls-in-bio-knit\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\"><strong>The Carry-All Set</strong></a><br />\nThe Carry-All Set includes 3 multipurpose draw-string pouches. Perfect as a “clutch” for quick errands, to organize toiletries and swimsuits when traveling, storage for fresh produce (goodbye disposable plastic bags!), or even as additional storage inside of your other Junes bags. The Terracotta shade is perfect for fall, but there’s a <a title=\"variety of color options\" href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes/products/carry-alls-in-bio-knit\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">variety of color options</a> to choose from.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes/products/grande-tote\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone wp-image-460712 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_grandetote_1280x900-810x570.jpg\" alt=\"woman carrying black junes grande tote over her shoulder\" width=\"810\" height=\"570\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_grandetote_1280x900-810x570.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_grandetote_1280x900-800x563.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_grandetote_1280x900-768x540.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/junes_grandetote_1280x900.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong><a title=\"The Grande Tote\" href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/junes/products/grande-tote\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">The Grande Tote</a></strong><br />\nAs the name suggests, this bag is absolutely massive – which self-proclaimed bag ladies like me will love. The Grande Tote is ideal for farmer’s market hauls, beach trips (it fits two towels with room to spare), or weekend getaways. Trust that the durable straps on the Grande Tote can hold their weight, the bag can carry up to 35lbs!</p>\n<p><strong>&#62;&#62;&#62; For more from Junes, click <a title=\"here\" 00:55:18","updatedTime":"2021-09-28 00:55:18","title":"The Quirk Hotel Charlottesville Serves as a Blank Canvas for Local Art + Culture","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=460470","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/the-quirk-hotel-charlottesville-serves-as-a-blank-canvas-for-local-art-culture/architecturefirm-quirk-hotel-charlottesville-11/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/architecturefirm-quirk-hotel-charlottesville-11-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"The Quirk Hotel Charlottesville Serves as a Blank Canvas for Local Art + Culture\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Designed by <a href=\"https://www.architecturefirm.co/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><strong>ARCHITECTUREFIRM</strong></a>, the <a href=\"https://www.destinationhotels.com/quirk-charlottesville\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><strong>Quirk Hotel</strong></a>, in Charlottesville, Virginia was designed as a gallery hotel, one that prides itself on being a blank canvas to be filled with art by local artists that can then be appreciated by locals and travelers alike. Rather than creating an interior that would distract from the art, ARCHITECTUREFIRM kept the interiors simple with clean white walls and let the architecture of the building shine through.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460474\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460474\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-460474\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/architecturefirm-quirk-hotel-charlottesville-4-810x1013.jpg\" alt=\"modern hotel\" width=\"810\" height=\"1013\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/architecturefirm-quirk-hotel-charlottesville-4-810x1013.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/architecturefirm-quirk-hotel-charlottesville-4-800x1000.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/architecturefirm-quirk-hotel-charlottesville-4-768x960.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/architecturefirm-quirk-hotel-charlottesville-4-1229x1536.jpg 1229w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/architecturefirm-quirk-hotel-charlottesville-4.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Even from the street, one can detect the beauty and drama of the lobby, which features a series of split arches that serve as the organization and wayfinding through the lobby. Each set of arches direct guests to the other spaces off the main lobby, including the restaurant, ballrooms and elevator lobby to take guests to their rooms or the rooftop bars. The lobby also consists of the front desk, a lobby bar, multiple lounge spaces and a retail shop.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=460483\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-460483\" Hoek’s modern Home Office Desk makes for the ideal workspace with its sleek and contemporary design. Optional shelving offers ergonomic laptop visibility or bonus storage, and its high-quality materials don’t feel like an afterthought. Everything about Hoek’s desk is carefully considered and a favorite feature is its <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/hoek-is-sustainable-furniture-built-in-60-seconds/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">effortless assembly</a> and take down for seamless storage if you’re tight on space. After many furniture-induced meltdowns, the ability to build and pack away in a pinch is priceless!</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/products/orbitkey-desk-mat\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone wp-image-460381 size-full\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/orbitkey_deskmat_design-milk-shop-810x540-1.jpg\" alt=\"orbitkey desk mat with keyboard, mouse, and cable organizer in a work from home set up\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/orbitkey_deskmat_design-milk-shop-810x540-1.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/orbitkey_deskmat_design-milk-shop-810x540-1-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/09/orbitkey_deskmat_design-milk-shop-810x540-1-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a title=\"Desk Mat by Orbitkey\" href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/products/orbitkey-desk-mat\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\"><strong>Desk Mat by Orbitkey</strong></a><br />\nThis Desk Mat by Orbitkey is a must for prolonging the lifespan of your workspace, and if you’re like me, preventing any dreaded coffee rings (the vegan leather material repels water and can be easily wiped clean).
